texlive-alegreya in fedora-32

This page displays detail informations of the texlive-alegreya package. You might want go back to the main page of texlive-alegreya.

Changelog

Date Author Change
2020-03-05 Tom Callaway - 9:2019-19 - drop Requires: stix-fonts stix-math-fonts from texlive-stix (bz1806271) this was more of a courtesy requires, but now that stix-fonts is 2.0, totally unnecessary
2020-02-01 Tom Callaway - 9:2019-18 - update newtx to latest upstream from CTAN to resolve naming issue with ntxsups_T1.enc
2020-01-31 Fedora Release Engineering - 9:2019-17 - Rebuilt for https://fedoraproject.org/wiki/Fedora_32_Mass_Rebuild
2020-01-22 Tom Callaway - 9:2019-16 - drop texlive-texinfo, Fedora uses newer files in texinfo-tex instead (bz1793993)
2020-01-14 Tom Callaway - 9:2019-15 - fix texlive-kerkis to only include the type1 kerkis fonts, not all of the type1 fonts in texlive (bz1790867) - properly package up the type1 fonts which were previously only in texlive-kerkis
2020-01-13 Tom Callaway - 9:2019-14 - update noto to resolve issue with missing .enc file - update noto provides to reflect current state
2020-01-07 Tom Callaway - 9:2019-13 - add Requires: texlive-platex to texlive-platex-tools (bz1785793)
2020-01-06 Tom Callaway - 9:2019-12 - fix dependencies for texlive-acmart (bz1787181)
2019-12-11 Tom Callaway - 9:2019-11 - patch tabu to latest git code to fix doxygen issues
2019-12-09 Tom Callaway - 9:2019-10 - add versioned Requires on biber for texlive-biblatex - add packager notes around biblatex
